event = {
id = 700006
random = no
country = RUS
style = 2

atwar = no
}

date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1937 }
offset = 1000
deathdate = { day = 1 month = january year = 1960 }

picture = "russiageo"

name = "Nikolai Trubetskoy Publishes 'Principles of Geopolitics'"
desc = "'Princypiya geopolitiki', published in the late 30's by Nikolai Trubetskoy, is now considered a cornerstone of modern geopolitics. In his book the Russian conservative philosopher and politician envisioned a new Russian Empire. Defined not by the Tsardom or religion but rather by pragmatic control over the Eurasian continent. His ideas were further developed by Lev Gumilov thus creating the so-called Eurasian Doctrine."

action_a = {
name = "An interesting concept indeed!"
command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
}
}

# Presidental election
# 1937
event = {
id = 759435
random = no
country = RUS
style = 2

trigger = {
flag = RUS_REP
NOT = { headofstate = 4193 } # Dmitri Romanov, since he gets officially elected in 1936
}

id = 758086
random = no
country = RUS
style = 2

trigger = {
flag = RUS_IND
flag = RUS_STATEECO
}

name = "First Year of Industrialisation"
desc = "Our intensive industrialisation programme has produced first results."
picture = "russianindustry"

date = { day = 1 month = december year = 1937 }
offset = 2
deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1937 }


action_a = {
name = "A modern state needs a good industrial base"
command = { type = construct which = ic where = 572 value = 2 }
command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 572 value = 10 }
command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 553 value = 20 }
command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 589 value = 20 }
command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 663 value = 20 }
command = {  type = supplies value = -400  }
command = { type = sleepevent which = 758091 }
command = { type = sleepevent which = 758096 }
command = { type = sleepevent which = 758101 }
}
}

}

offset = 2

############################
# Science Funding & Upgrading Nuclear Team
############################
event = {
id = 758106
random = no
country = RUS

trigger = {
	random = 10
		OR = {
		incabinet = 4416 #Vladimir Ipatiev
		incabinet = 4362 #Boris Stechkin
		incabinet = 4231 #Andrei D. Sakharov
		incabinet = 4422 #Yakov Kolotyrkin
		incabinet = 4478 #Vladimir Kotelnikov
		}
	NOT = {
	event = 758107
	}
}

name = "Additional science funding"
desc = "Our minister of armament has proposed to organise a national support programme for our scientists. Even though many mundane people consider this a waste of funds, it is believed that further empirical research may lead to interesting results."
style = 2
picture = "invest_research"

date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
offset = 30
deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1970 }

action_a = {
	ai_chance = 40
	name = "Invest into physics and mathematics."
	command = { type = money value = -250 }
